Everything is expensive, rent, wages, accounting, taxes, insurance, workers comp, tools, equipments, parts, warranty... just endless items we need to pay. We wish we can charge customers less, but so far, while everybody is always busy working, we still struggle to to pay all the bills. Often times, especially with older cars, frequently, when one problem is repaired, other problems appeared. This is due to the the aging of all parts of the car. When work on older cars, in the process of removing and installing certain parts, surrounding parts, especially parts like aging wiring, hoses, sensors may fail without warning. Therefore, what we can do is to professional diagnose and fix a problem that is obvious, other problems that may emerge after the fix is beyond our responsibility, unless it is clearly caused by a mistake we made. < Text>
Stop reading past this review and just go there!

Order anything and it's amazing. It's all homemade recipes with Mama May and Lil May. Ribs, love em. Chicken, delish. Specials... I advise you try them. Also, grab a cup of Peach Sweet Tea. Collard greens are amazing if you know what's good for ya, but all the sides are great.

Pricing is reasonable for some home cooking and seasoning made from pure love. I don't want to know their secrets because I want them to stay a staple in the community.

Ignore the old reviews from past owners, and just try it for yourself. Parking in front is limited,but there's always street parking nearby.

Worst thing that can happen is you end up spending more than you thought because you're busy ordering the entire menu and returning to them spending more for another outstanding meal.

The meal in the picture was a fried chicken sandwich with coleslaw and a sweet sauce. Sides of crawfish mac n cheese, collard greens, and potato salad. Across the way is BBQ chicken with the top notch sauce. Peach tea all around and the best desert you can imagine after... Honey bourbon corn bread!

I love this place and I love these two amazing women. Their customer service is top notch. Have a chat, tell a story, get a hug, and leave happy!<//Text>

<username>Julianne Pohl< /username>< text>
I got take-out for the first time about a month ago, and my husband and I loved it!  I got the pork ribs and beef brisket, macaroni & cheese, collard greens and corn bread. The meats were tender, juicy, and smoked perfectly, and the sauce and seasonings complimented the meat well; some places I go overpower the meat with theirs. The mac & cheese was creamy and had a nice hint of garlic. The collard greens were traditionally prepared, so very tender and smoky. The cornbread was almost like cake - soft and honey-sweetened. They seemed a bit pricey, but good food like this takes time and effort. I'll definitely be back!<//text>

< Text>
If Jesus had BBQ at the last supper, he would have ordered it from The Famous Rib Shack. Mama May and Little May make the best ribs I've ever eaten, and I try every BBQ joint I pass. They converted my fianc√© from a rib skeptic to a rib nut.

Other reviews say FRS is slow or expensive, but guys, have you ever eaten Barbeque before?!?!?! There is no such thing as cheap or fast BBQ (if it's good). If you're in a hurry that day, don't eat BBQ. This stuff is made with pure love, and love takes time.

Treat yourself to some of the May's finest cooking, and their southern hospitality. You'll feel like you stepped right back into your momma's kitchen, except your mother never made anything so delicious as Mama May's barbeque.</Text>

< review>
We were driving by the other night and saw this place and decided to check it out, they were closed but the owner Lottie invited us in to look around and "I'll give you a sample!"
The sample was SOOOO good we came back tonight for dinner.  I love baby back ribs and my wife loves beef ribs.  We got both. The pork ribs were succulent, flavorful and some of the best I have ever had, the beef ribs were HUGE, cooked erfectly and delicious.  Both the mild sauce and the hot sauce (we got them on the side) were terrific but we liked the hot a bit more.. The corn bread was out of this world as were the sides. Collard greens with flecks of ham, macaroni & cheese, coleslaw.  We left stuffed and with doggie bags.  We will be back for sure. The food was great, the owner is a sweetheart and the service was wonderful.< /review>

<Time>1493525951277<//Time><Rate>4<//Rate>< Text>
This place a is a little hard to rate.

Food is great.
Service is slow but very friendly (Not enough staff)
Restaurant is small but clean, not enough parking.
Cheapest menu item is around $12 and 3 ribs around $16. They ribs and bbq sauce are great so the amount you pay for the food is worth it. However, when you realize that you spent $50 for two ribs sets of 3 and 2 drinks + tips it makes you think about other local alternatives (Olive Garden, BJs, chillis).

- if you are craving some good ribs and dont care about the location or you are not in a rush this is the place to go.< /Text>

It was completely cut off from the world -- a little slice of paradise that you could usually have all to yourself. Now, it seems as though it has been developed. <Rating>5< /Rating><Review>Excellent fairly strenuous hike with amazing views of Vandenberg airforce base to the South (On clear days you can even see the oil platforms off the coast near Goleta) and Pismo and Avila to the North. Stay on the trail as the beginning of the hike is on private property and at the top of the hill is Vandenberg property. No facilities and be sure to bring lots of water especially if you decide to go all the way down to the beach as coming back up the hill can be quite difficult especially at midday, I have seen bikes here but am not sure if they are allowed. Dogs can be on leash. As the parking location is a bit isolated be sure to not leave any valuables in your car or carry them with you. My car has been broken in here and I think it happens pretty often as I have seen window glass several times.<//Review>< user>

<time>1513384456673</time><Name>Roland Raga</Name><Text>After several months I am finally writing this review for this amazing establishment.  I came here, with my girlfiend, around July to attend the diamond class that they offer.  I literally knew nothing when it came to diamonds (they all sort of looked the same to me) but Shawn was very diligent in informing us about the basics of diamonds and how they are categorized.  She tailored the lesson as we went along to discuss topics that we had more interest in.  It really felt like a class!  We compared sizes, colors and clarity of diamonds and she brings out examples to compare, giving us a clearer picture of the topics she was explaining.  The class itself is very in depth and informative, it ultimately helped me make a choice for my purchase of an engagement ring.

I came back a few months later in September I emailed The Classic Rock and made an appointment to come in, hoping to get the process started on choosing an engagement ring within the one hour I had prior to work.  The staff is very welcoming and attentive to all of your ideas and requests, as well as your time constraints!  Ruth had brought up the information that was written down during the diamond class we took in July so it was easy to choose a round cut, but she helped me decide what diamond size range I wanted to go with.  After this visit they had ordered a few diamonds that fit the criteria we discussed within my one hour visit.

A few days later the diamonds arrive and I am again at the store deciding between carat weights of the selected diamonds that fit the criteria I chose.  It was such a simple process as Ruth, Shawn and Jeanne provide input on all the pro's and cons between the diamonds in terms of different aspects of the diamonds themselves.  I thought I'd have a little more stress in this choosing process but it was so simple coming here. I went with a 1.51 carat VS2 F clarity round cut!  I cannot stress how simple it was to get this process started and for them to work around my time constraints and take into consideration my budget.  My ring was basically done; my diamond was chosen, the band was chosen and I just had one last request.  I wanted to add a little detail to the band and requested to place a small sapphire stone on one side of the band so only she could see it.  Ruth took the request and made it happen!  She gave an example of the finished product while the ring was being put together and I was overly satisfied with the result.

Fast forward 4-6 weeks in October later and the ring was finished.  I pretended to go to the gym but I really picked up the ring!  Fast forward again to November at the Conservatory of Flowers in SF where I proposed to my girlfriend.  She said yes of course!  All thanks to The Classic Rock.  I still cannot believe how easy they made it for me to choose a ring.  I highly recommend this place to any guy looking to purchase an engagement ring.  I promise it isn't as scary as you'd think, as long as you come here!</Text><pictures>None</pictures>< userid>

The Albertsons has a stand alone cooler with sushi that is made fresh daily. While I don't care for sushi my girlfriend loves the stuff. Renting the truck from Home Depot is super easy!< /review>

All entrances into this shopping center are off center! You enter from Lomita Blvd and like 20 feet after entering, you have to stop for cross traffic because they don't have a stop. It should be the other way around. The shopping center has good stores. Home Depot, Staples and a supermarket that is very clean and quite large! There are fast food restaurants on the East corner and parking there is very tight and difficult! There's an awkwardly placed gas station and getting in and out of it is like a game of chicken.
